 mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image099.png"
  o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=741 height=417
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image100.jpg" v:shapes="Image_x0020_70"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l32 level1 lfo25'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Warning: The button &#8220;Reset&#8221;
at the very bottom part of the &#8220;Project administration&#8221; panel
restart the pipeline from scratch removing all configurations previously set up
and all data and result files generated.</span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc62127971"><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>5.4.7 Step
7: Prior-scenario checking PRE-ANALYSIS (optional but recommended)</span></a><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoBodyText><span lang=EN-US>Before performing a full ABC-RF analysis
on a large size training set, we advise using the prior-scenario checking
option on a training set of small size (e.g. including 500 to 1000 simulated
dataset per scenarios). As a matter of fact, this pre-analysis option is a
convenient way to reveal potential mis-specification of models (scenarios)
and/or prior distributions of parameters (and correct it). This action requires
a training set file (`<span class=SpellE>reftableRF.bin</span>`) and a
statobsRF.txt file either generated when clicking on 'Simulate' or uploaded
with an existing project. When clicking on the button <u>&#8220;Run&#8221; of
the &#8220;Prior and scenario checking&#8221; option (see previous/above panel
copy)</u> the program will use the statobsRF.txt and <span class=SpellE>reftableRF.bin</span>
files to generate two specific outputs:</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l12 level1 lfo28'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>A Principal Component Analysis
(PCA) representing on 2-axes plans the simulated dataset from the training set
and the observed dataset as graphical output. Note that this figure is somewhat
similar in its spirit to the graphical output
LDA_training_set_and_obs_dataset.png obtained when running the scenario choice
option in &#8220;Random Forest Analyses&#8221;. The latter output is different,
however, as it corresponds to the projection of the datasets from the training
set linear discriminant analysis (LDA) axes (see section 7.3 for details).</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l12 level1 lfo28'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>A numerical output file, named
pcaloc1_locate.txt, which includes for each summary statistics and for each
scenario, the proportion of simulated data (considering the total training set)
that have a summary statistics value below the value of the observed dataset. A
star indicates proportions lower than 5% or greater than 95% (two stars, &lt;1%
or &gt;1%; three stars, &lt;0.1% or &gt;0.1%). The presence of such star
symbols is a sign of substantial mismatch between the observed dataset and the
simulated datasets. The latter numerical results can help users to
reformulating the compared scenarios and/or the associated prior distributions
in order to achieve some compatibility (see e.g. <span class=SpellE>Cornuet</span>
et al. 2010). If only a few stars are observed at a few summary statistics for
one or several scenarios, one can conclude that prior-scenario conditions are
suitable enough to further process Random Forest analysis, and this potentially
on a training set including more simulated datasets.</span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc62127972"><span lang=EN-US>5.5 How to generate a new </span></a><span
class=SpellE><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc62127972'><span lang=EN-US>PoolSeq</span></span></span><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc62127972'><span lang=EN-US> SNP training set</span></span></h2>

<p class=MsoBodyText><span lang=EN-US>Follow the same five steps described in
section 5.4 for <span class=SpellE>IndSeq</span> SNPs.</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l15 level1 lfo18'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span
lang=EN-US>Step 1</span></i><span lang=EN-US>: Defining a new <span
class=SpellE>PoolSeq</span> SNP project </span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:
Wingdings'>&agrave;</span><span lang=EN-US> see section 5.4.1 </span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText><span lang=EN-US>Click on the &#8220;Launch project&#8221;
button of the home screen. Select SNP as project type and <span class=SpellE>PoolSeq</span>
as sequencing mode </span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l15 level1 lfo18'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span
lang=EN-US>Step 2</span></i><span lang=EN-US>: Choosing the data file </span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;
mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings'>&agrave;</span><span lang=EN-US> see section
5.4.2 and select a dataset file characterized by a <span class=SpellE>PoolSeq</span>
format (format detailed in section 7.1.2).</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l15 level1 lfo18'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span
lang=EN-US>Step 3</span></i><span lang=EN-US>: Inform the Historical model </span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;
mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings'>&agrave;</span><span lang=EN-US> see section
5.4.3 </span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l15 level1 lfo18'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span
lang=EN-US>Step 4</span></i><span lang=EN-US>: Inform chromosome type and
number of loci </span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:
Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings'>&agrave;</span><span lang=EN-US> see
section 5.4.4 </span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText><span lang=EN-US>Note: The panel for <span class=SpellE>PoolSeq</span>
SNPs is simpler than for <span class=SpellE>IndSeq</span> SNPs because <span
class=SpellE>PoolSeq</span> SNPs are considered as located on <b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>autosomal chromosomes only</b>.</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l44 level1 lfo21'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span
lang=EN-US>Step 5</span></i><span lang=EN-US>: Summary statistics: </span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;
mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings'>&agrave;</span><span lang=EN-US> see section
5.4.5</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l44 level1 lfo21'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span
lang=EN-US>Step 6</span></i><span lang=EN-US>: Simulate the training set </span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;
mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings'>&agrave;</span><span lang=EN-US> see section
5.4.6 </span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l44 level1 lfo21'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span
lang=EN-US>Step 7</span></i><span lang=EN-US> (optional but recommended):
Prior-scenario checking PRE-ANALYSIS </span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings'>&agrave;</span><span
lang=EN-US> see section 5.4.7</span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc62127973"><span lang=EN-US>5.6 How to generate a new
microsatellite (and/or DNA sequence) training set</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoBodyText><span lang=EN-US>Follow the same steps described in
section 5.4 for <span class=SpellE>IndSeq</span> SNPs.</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l15 level1 lfo18'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span
lang=EN-US>Step 1</span></i><span lang=EN-US>: Defining a new or
microsatellites/DNA sequences project </span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings'>&agrave;</span><span
lang=EN-US> see section 5.4.1 </span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt'><span lang=EN-US>Click on the
&#8220;Launch project&#8221; button of the home screen. Select <span
class=SpellE>Microsat</span>/Sequences as project type (not any sequencing mode
is needed)</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l15 level1 lfo18'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span
lang=EN-US>Step 2</span></i><span lang=EN-US>: Choosing the data file </span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;
mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings'>&agrave;</span><span lang=EN-US> see section
5.4.2 and select a dataset file characterized by a Microsatellite and/or DNA
Sequences format (format detailed in section 7.1.3).</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l15 level1 lfo18'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span
lang=EN-US>Step 3</span></i><span lang=EN-US>: Inform the Historical model </span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;
mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings'>&agrave;</span><span lang=EN-US> see section
5.4.3 </span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l15 level1 lfo18'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><i
style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US>Step 4</span></i><span
lang=EN-US>: The panel &#8220;Inform chromosome type and number of loci&#8221;
is replaced by the panel &#8220;Inform the genetic model&#8221; </span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Wingdings;
mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings'>&agrave;</span><span
lang=EN-US> see details below in section 5.6.1</span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l44 level1 lfo21'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><i
style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US>Step 5</span></i><span
lang=EN-US>: Summary statistics: different sets of summary statistics are
computed as compared to SNP summary statistics </span></b><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:
Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings'>&agrave;</span><span lang=EN-US> see
details below in section 5.6.2<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l44 level1 lfo21'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span
lang=EN-US>Step 6</span></i><span lang=EN-US>: Simulate the training set </span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;
mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings'>&agrave;</span><span lang=EN-US> see section
5.4.6 </span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l44 level1 lfo21'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span
lang=EN-US>Step 7</span></i><span lang=EN-US> (optional but recommended):
Prior-scenario checking PRE-ANALYSIS </span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings'>&agrave;</span><span
lang=EN-US> see section 5.4.7</span></p>

<h3 style='margin-left:18.0pt'><a name="_Toc62127974"><span lang=EN-US>5.6.1
Step 4: Inform the genetic model</span></a><span lang=EN-US> </span></h3>

<p class=FirstParagraph style='margin-left:36.0pt'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><u><span lang=EN-US>For microsatellite markers</span></u><span
lang=EN-US>: Informing the genetic model can be done using the following panels
(implemented here from a toy example including microsatellites + DNA sequences named
TOY_EXAMPLE2_microsatellites_DNAsequence_two_pops_ancient_admixture; see
section 10. TOY EXAMPLES for details about this toy example).<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l44 level1 lfo21'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>First:<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>define the number of groups of markers
(a group been defined by different mutational modalities). By default, all
microsatellite loci are grouped together, same for all DNA sequence loci. If
you want to define more than a single group then <span class=help-block>configure
the number of groups (<span class=SpellE>cf</span> button &#8220;Add
group&#8221;) and then assign each locus to one of those groups using the Group
arrow on the right.</span></span></p>

<p class=FirstParagraph><span style='mso-ansi-language:FR;mso-fareast-language:
FR;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Image_x0020_16" o:spid="_x0000_i1048"
 type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:442.2pt;height:248.4pt;visibility:visible;
 mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image101.png"
  o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=590 height=331
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image102.jpg" v:shapes="Image_x0020_16"><![endif]></span><span
style='mso-ansi-language:FR;mso-fareast-language:FR'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=FirstParagraph style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;
mso-list:l26 level1 lfo35'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-language:FR'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:FR'>Second: define the motif size and
range of motif variation. </span><span class=help-block><span lang=EN-US>By
default, all microsatellite loci are supposed to be <span class=SpellE>dinucleotidic</span>
(motif = 2) with a range of 40.</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
FR'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText><span style='mso-ansi-language:FR;mso-fareast-language:
FR;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Image_x0020_17" o:spid="_x0000_i1047"
 type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:440.4pt;height:247.8pt;visibility:visible;
 mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image103.png"
  o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=587 height=330
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image104.jpg" v:shapes="Image_x0020_17"><![endif]></span><span
style='mso-ansi-language:FR;mso-fareast-language:FR'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt'><span lang=EN-US>It is worth
stressing that the values for motif size and allelic range are just default
values and do not necessarily correspond to the actual data. The user who knows
the real values for its data is required to set the correct values at this
stage. If the range is too short to include all values observed in the analyzed
dataset, a message appears in a box asking to enlarge the corresponding allelic
range. Note that the allelic range is measured in number of motifs, so that a
range of 40 for a motif length of 2 bp means that the difference between the
smallest and the longest alleles should not exceed 80 bp. It is worth stressing
that the indicated allelic range (expressed in number of continuous allelic
states) corresponds to a potential range which is usually larger than the range
observed from the analyzed dataset (cf.&nbsp;all possible allelic states have usually
not been sampled). In practice it is difficult to assess the actual
microsatellite constraints on the allelic range; to do that one needs allelic
data from several distantly related populations/sub-species as well as related
species which is rarely the case(see Pollack et al. 1998; Estoup et al. 2002).
We achieved a meta-analysis from numerous primer notes documenting the
microsatellite allelic ranges of many (i.e.&nbsp;&gt; 100) different species
(and related species). We used the corrective statistical treatment on such
data proposed by (Pollack et al. 1998). Our results pointed to a mean
microsatellite allelic range of 40 continuous states (hence the default allelic
range value of 40 mentioned in the program). We also found, however, that range
values greatly varied among species and among loci within species (unpublished
results). We therefore recommend the following pragmatic behavior when
considering the allelic range of your <span class=SpellE>analysed</span>
microsatellite dataset: (<span class=SpellE>i</span>) if the difference in
number of motif of your locus is &lt; 40 motifs in the <span class=SpellE>analysed</span>
dataset then leave the default allelic range value of 40. (ii) if the
difference in number of motif of your locus is &gt;40 motifs in your dataset
then take <span class=SpellE>Max_allele_size</span> </span><!--[if gte msEquation 12]><m:oMath><i
 style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Cambria Math",serif'><m:r>-</m:r></span></i></m:oMath><![endif]--><![if !msEquation]><span
style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:107%;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-bidi;
position:relative;top:2.5pt;mso-text-raise:-2.5pt;mso-ansi-language:FR;
mso-fareast-language:FR;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="_x0000_i1025" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:9pt;height:22.8pt'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image105.png"
  o:title="" chromakey="white"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=12 height=30
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image106.gif" v:shapes="_x0000_i1025"><![endif]></span><![endif]><span
lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span>Min_allele_size)/motif
size + say 10 additi<span class=SpellE>onal</span> motifs to re-define the
allelic range of the locus in the corresponding DIYABC panel (e.g.&nbsp;(200 nu
</span><!--[if gte msEquation 12]><m:oMath><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span
 lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Cambria Math",serif'><m:r>-</m:r></span></i></m:oMath><![endif]--><![if !msEquation]><span
style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:107%;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-bidi;
position:relative;top:2.5pt;mso-text-raise:-2.5pt;mso-ansi-language:FR;
mso-fareast-language:FR;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="_x0000_i1025" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:9pt;height:22.8pt'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image105.png"
  o:title="" chromakey="white"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=12 height=30
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image106.gif" v:shapes="_x0000_i1025"><![endif]></span><![endif]><span
lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span>100 <span class=GramE>nu</span>)/2
+ 10 = 50 + 10 = 60 as allelic range).</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l26 level1 lfo35'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Third: adjust the prior
specificities of mutational modalities as you want using the corresponding buttons
in the panel below. Otherwise keep the default values as the latter have been
reported for many eukaryote species (e.g. Estoup et al. 2002; but see <span
class=SpellE>Fraimout</span> et al. 2017).</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText><span style='mso-ansi-language:FR;mso-fareast-language:
FR;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Image_x0020_19" o:spid="_x0000_i1046"
 type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:555.6pt;height:312.6pt;visibility:visible;
 mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image107.png"
  o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=741 height=417
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image108.jpg" v:shapes="Image_x0020_19"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=FirstParagraph><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><u><span
lang=EN-US><o:p><span style='text-decoration:none'>&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></u></b></p>

<p class=FirstParagraph><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><u><span
lang=EN-US>For DNA sequence markers</span></u><span lang=EN-US>: Informing the
genetic model can be done using the following panels (implemented here from the
same toy example as above). <o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l44 level1 lfo21'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>We need to define at least one
group of DNA sequence loci. </span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt'><span style='mso-ansi-language:
FR;mso-fareast-language:FR;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Image_x0020_18"
 o:spid="_x0000_i1045" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:555.6pt;height:312.6pt;
 visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image109.png"
  o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=741 height=417
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image110.jpg" v:shapes="Image_x0020_18"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l44 level1 lfo21'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Suppose that we want all DNA
sequence loci in the same group because we consider that they all have similar
mutational modalities. We then put &#8220;2&#8221; in the button
&#8220;Group&#8221; for all loci (Group 1 is for the previous microsatellite
markers). Otherwise you can associate some loci to additional groups (after
clicking on the button &#8220;Add group&#8221;) if you consider that such loci
have different mutational modalities (for instance here Locus_S_M_16_).</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l44 level1 lfo21'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Adjust the prior specificities
of mutational modalities (for the different DNA sequence groups you have
defined previously) using the corresponding buttons in the panel below.
Otherwise keep the default values as the latter have been reported for many
eukaryote species (e.g. <span class=SpellE>Cornuet</span> et al. 2010).</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:18.0pt'><span style='mso-ansi-language:
FR;mso-fareast-language:FR;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Image_x0020_21"
 o:spid="_x0000_i1044" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:510pt;height:286.8pt;
 visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image111.png"
  o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=680 height=382
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image112.jpg" v:shapes="Image_x0020_21"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt'><span lang=EN-US>The default
values are indicated in the panel. Note that the default mean mutation rate is
not suited to mitochondrial DNA which generally evolves at a faster rate than
nuclear DNA (Haag-<span class=SpellE>Liautard</span> et al., 2008). <span
class=GramE>So</span> we set its value to 10<sup>-8</sup>. For all other
mutation model parameters, one can just keep the default values. <u>See section
2.4.2 &#8220;DNA sequence loci&#8221; for details about the mutation models
proposed for DNA sequences</u>.</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l44 level1 lfo21'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-language:
FR'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
FR'>Before launching a run to simulate the training set, do not forget to <u>validate
your microsatellite and/or DNA settings by clicking on the blue-color button
&#8220;Validate&#8221;</u>. Indicate the number of simulations in the
corresponding button (here 30000) and click on the button
&#8220;Simulate&#8221; to launch the simulation of the training set.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText><span style='mso-ansi-language:FR;mso-fareast-language:
FR;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Image_x0020_22" o:spid="_x0000_i1043"
 type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:457.8pt;height:256.8pt;visibility:visible;
 mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image113.png"
  o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=610 height=342
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image114.jpg" v:shapes="Image_x0020_22"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc62127975"><span lang=EN-US>5.6.2 Step 5: Summary statistics</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:2.85pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span lang=EN-US>In the present
version of the program, <u>all</u> available summary statistics are computed as
mentioned in the interface below the &#8220;Summary statistics&#8221; item (see
previous panel-copy) and as detailed when clicking on the button &#8220;?&#8221;
on the right:<span style='color:black;mso-themecolor:text1;background:yellow;
mso-highlight:yellow'><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><u><span
lang=EN-US>For microsatellite loci<o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:2.85pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span lang=EN-US>The following set of
summary statistics has been implemented. </span></p>

<p class=DefinitionTerm><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=DefinitionTerm><span lang=EN-US>Single sample statistics:</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US>1. mean number of alleles across loci (NAL)</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US>2. mean gene diversity across loci (HET)</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US>3. mean allele size variance across loci (VAR)</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>3. mean M index across loci (MGW)</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=DefinitionTerm><span lang=EN-US>Two sample statistics:</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US>1. mean number of alleles across loci (two samples) (N2P)</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US>2. mean gene diversity across loci (two samples) (H2P)</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US>3. mean allele size variance across loci (two samples) (V2P)</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><!--[if gte msEquation 12]><m:oMath><m:sSub><m:sSubPr><span
   style='font-family:"Cambria Math",serif;mso-ascii-font-family:"Cambria Math";
   mso-hansi-font-family:"Cambria Math"'><m:ctrlPr></m:ctrlPr></span></m:sSubPr><m:e><i
   style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Cambria Math",serif'><m:r>3.</m:r><m:r>F</m:r></span></i></m:e><m:sub><i
   style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Cambria Math",serif'><m:r>ST</m:r></span></i></m:sub></m:sSub></m:oMath><![endif]--><![if !msEquation]><span
style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:107%;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-bidi;
position:relative;top:2.5pt;mso-text-raise:-2.5pt;mso-ansi-language:FR;
mso-fareast-language:FR;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="_x0000_i1025" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:27.6pt;height:13.8pt'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image115.png"
  o:title="" chromakey="white"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=37 height=18
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image116.gif" v:shapes="_x0000_i1025"><![endif]></span><![endif]><span
lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span>between two samples
(FST)</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US>4. mean index of classification (two samples) (LIK)</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US>5. shared allele distance between two samples (DAS)</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Cambria;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast'>6.</span><span
lang=EN-US> distance between two samples (DM2)</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=DefinitionTerm><span lang=EN-US>Three sample statistics:</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US>1. Maximum likelihood coefficient of admixture (AML)</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><u><span
lang=EN-US><o:p><span style='text-decoration:none'>&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></u></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><u><span
lang=EN-US>For DNA sequence loci<o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:2.85pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span lang=EN-US>The following set of
summary statistics has been implemented. </span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=DefinitionTerm><span lang=EN-US>Single sample statistics:</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US>1. number of distinct haplotypes (NHA)</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US>2. number of segregating sites (NSS)</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US>3. mean pairwise difference (MPD)</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US>4. variance of the number of pairwise differences (VPD)</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US>5. Tajima&#8217;s D statistics (DTA)</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US>6. Number of private segregating sites (PSS)</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US>7. Mean of the numbers of the rarest nucleotide at segregating sites
(MNS)</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US>8. Variance of the numbers of the rarest nucleotide at segregating
sites (VNS)</span></p>

<p class=DefinitionTerm><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=DefinitionTerm><span lang=EN-US>Two sample statistics:</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US>1. number of distinct haplotypes in the pooled sample (NH2)</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US>2. number of segregating sites in the pooled sample (NS2)</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US>3. mean of within sample pairwise differences (MP2)</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US>4. mean of between sample pairwise differences (MPB)</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Cambria;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span></span><!--[if gte msEquation 12]><m:oMath><m:sSub><m:sSubPr><span
   style='font-family:"Cambria Math",serif;mso-ascii-font-family:"Cambria Math";
   mso-hansi-font-family:"Cambria Math"'><m:ctrlPr></m:ctrlPr></span></m:sSubPr><m:e><i
   style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Cambria Math",serif'><m:r>5.</m:r><m:r>F</m:r></span></i></m:e><m:sub><i
   style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Cambria Math",serif'><m:r>ST</m:r></span></i></m:sub></m:sSub></m:oMath><![endif]--><![if !msEquation]><span
style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:107%;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-bidi;
position:relative;top:2.5pt;mso-text-raise:-2.5pt;mso-ansi-language:FR;
mso-fareast-language:FR;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="_x0000_i1025" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:27.6pt;height:13.8pt'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image117.png"
  o:title="" chromakey="white"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=37 height=18
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image118.gif" v:shapes="_x0000_i1025"><![endif]></span><![endif]><span
lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span>between two samples
(HST)</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=DefinitionTerm style='margin-left:2.85pt'><span lang=EN-US>Three
sample statistics:</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:60.0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l9 level2 lfo10;
tab-stops:list 36.0pt'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-family:
Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>1.<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Maximum likelihood coefficient
of admixture (SML)</span></p>

<p class=Definition style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span
lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:
0cm;margin-left:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-pagination:widow-orphan lines-together;
page-break-after:avoid;mso-outline-level:2'><a name="_Toc62127976"><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:
major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-fareast;
mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-bidi;color:#4F81BD;
mso-themecolor:accent1'>5.7 How to work from an &#8220;Existing project&#8221;
(for any type of markers)</span></b></a><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
14.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-fareast;
mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-bidi;color:#4F81BD;
mso-themecolor:accent1'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:9.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:9.0pt;
margin-left:0cm'><span lang=EN-US>Working from an existing project is
particularly appealing when that one wants to:</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:9.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:9.0pt;
margin-left:0cm'><span lang=EN-US>(<span class=SpellE>i</span>) <b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>objective 1</b>: simply add more
simulations in the training set of the <span class=SpellE>reftableRF.bin</span>
of an existing project without changing anything in the headerRF.txt. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:9.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:9.0pt;
margin-left:0cm'><span lang=EN-US><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span>(ii) <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>objective
2</b>: use the headerRF.txt content of an existing project as a base to
generate a new headerRF.txt file including different changes for instance in
the scenarios formulated, in the definition of priors, the number of loci to
simulate&#8230;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:9.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:9.0pt;
margin-left:0cm'><span lang=EN-US>Let&#8217;s consider that one wants to work
from the <span class=SpellE>IndSeq_demonstration_project</span> previously
generated (and including a training set with 12000 simulation records) as
described in the above section 5.4.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-top:9.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:
9.0pt;margin-left:36.0pt;mso-add-space:auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l11 level1 lfo34'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Click on the &#8220;Start&#8221;
button in the middle of the Home panel. The following panel appears.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:9.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:9.0pt;
margin-left:0cm'><span style='mso-ansi-language:FR;mso-fareast-language:FR;
mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Image_x0020_23" o:spid="_x0000_i1042"
 type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:555.6pt;height:312.6pt;visibility:visible;
 mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image119.png"
  o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=741 height=417
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image120.jpg" v:shapes="Image_x0020_23"><![endif]></span></p>

<ul style='margin-top:0cm' type=disc>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:9.0pt;margin-bottom:9.0pt;mso-list:l6 level1 lfo32'><span
     lang=EN-US>Enter a project name in the &#8220;Project name&#8221; window
     (here &#8220;<span class=SpellE>Starting_from_existing_project_IndSeq_demonstration_project</span>&#8221;)
     and validate the project name.</span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:9.0pt;margin-bottom:9.0pt;mso-list:l6 level1 lfo32'><span
     lang=EN-US>Select the project type (<span class=SpellE>Microsat</span>/sequence
     or SNP) and the sequencing mode (for SNP only; <span class=SpellE>IndSeq</span>
     or <span class=SpellE>PoolSeq</span>). As we will start from a
     pre-existing <span class=SpellE>IndSeq</span> project, select SNP and
     Individual Seq.</span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:9.0pt;margin-bottom:9.0pt;mso-list:l6 level1 lfo32'><span
     lang=EN-US>Click on the &#8220;Existing project&#8221; button of <span
     class=GramE>the &#8221;Project</span> type&#8221; item as we want to work
     from an existing project.</span></li>
</ul>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l6 level1 lfo32'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;
mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol;color:black;
mso-themecolor:text1'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
lang=EN-US style='color:black;mso-themecolor:text1'>Use the browser of <span
class=GramE>the &#8221;Project</span> files&#8221; item to select key files in
the Existing project directory (here a directory named &#8220;<span
class=SpellE>IndSeq_demonstration_project</span>&#8221;). Key files are <u>headerRF.txt</u>
(mandatory), <span class=SpellE><u>reftableRF.bin</u></span> (if one simply
wants to add more simulations in the training set of the <span class=SpellE>reftableRF.bin</span>
of an existing project without changing anything in the headerRF.txt cf.
objective 1 above), and <u>statobsRF.txt</u> (optional). If the objective 2 is
concerned then only the file headerRF.txt is needed (avoid loading the <span
class=SpellE>reftableRF.bin</span> file as the latter might not <span
class=GramE>be in agreement</span> with the new headerRF.txt file that you will
generate). </span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;mso-bidi-font-family:
Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-bidi;color:black;mso-themecolor:text1'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText><span style='mso-ansi-language:FR;mso-fareast-language:
FR;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Image_x0020_31" o:spid="_x0000_i1041"
 type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:555.6pt;height:312.6pt;visibility:visible;
 mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image121.png"
  o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=741 height=417
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image122.jpg" v:shapes="Image_x0020_31"><![endif]></span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:
minor-bidi;color:black;mso-themecolor:text1'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ul style='margin-top:0cm' type=disc>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:9.0pt;margin-bottom:9.0pt;mso-list:l27 level1 lfo26'><span
     lang=EN-US>Browse and choose a data file (an <span class=SpellE>IndSeq</span>
     format data file in this case) in the &#8220;Data file&#8221; window (here
     INDSNP_sim_dataset_4POP_001.snp). A short summary of the specificities of
     the loaded datafile appears: here the total number of loci (30000), the
     minimum allele frequency chosen for simulation (MAF=0.05), the sex ratio
     indicated by the user (NM=1NF), the total number of individuals and
     populations, and finally the locus type and their corresponding numbers
     (A= autosomal, M=<span class=GramE>mitochondrial,&#8230;</span>; see
     section 7.1 for details about data file format).</span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:9.0pt;margin-bottom:9.0pt;mso-list:l27 level1 lfo26'><span
     lang=EN-US>A &#8220;Project set up is ok&#8221; message appears at the
     bottom of the panel if all items have gone correctly. You can then go the
     next steps by clicking on the large blue color &#8220;Training set
     simulation&#8221; &#8220;+&#8221; button&#8221;. The following panel
     appears.</span></li>
</ul>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:9.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:9.0pt;
margin-left:18.0pt'><span style='mso-ansi-language:FR;mso-fareast-language:
FR;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Image_x0020_40" o:spid="_x0000_i1040"
 type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:483.6pt;height:272.4pt;visibility:visible;
 mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image123.png"
  o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=645 height=363
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image124.jpg" v:shapes="Image_x0020_40"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:9.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:9.0pt;
margin-left:36.0pt'><span lang=EN-US>The panel displays all information
included in the headerRF.txt file (historical models, priors and conditions,
number of SNP loci to simulate). Warning: such information cannot be changed. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:9.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:9.0pt;
margin-left:36.0pt'><span lang=EN-US>To change information in the headerRF.txt
(cf. <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>objective 2</b>) click on the
&#8220;Edit configuration&#8221; button located at the top of the panel and changes
for instance the scenarios formulated, the definition of priors, the number of
loci to simulate etc. In this case a new <span class=SpellE>reftableRF.bin</span>
file will be generated from scratch following the instruction included in the
newly generated headerRF.txt file. </span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-top:9.0pt;margin-right:0cm;
margin-bottom:9.0pt;margin-left:36.0pt;mso-add-space:auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;
mso-list:l27 level1 lfo26'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Following <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'>objective 1</b>, you can launch new simulations that will be added to
those already present in the pre-existing training set (i.e. <span
class=SpellE>reftableRF.bin</span> file). As we have already 12000 simulations
in the initial <span class=SpellE>reftableRF.bin</span> file we put the number
of <span class=GramE>simulation</span> to a number &gt; 12000 (here 24000).
Then click on the large blue color button &#8220;Simulate&#8221;.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-top:9.0pt;margin-right:0cm;
margin-bottom:9.0pt;margin-left:36.0pt;mso-add-space:auto'><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-top:9.0pt;margin-right:0cm;
margin-bottom:9.0pt;margin-left:36.0pt;mso-add-space:auto'><span
style='mso-ansi-language:FR;mso-fareast-language:FR;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="Image_x0020_41" o:spid="_x0000_i1039" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:435pt;
 height:244.8pt;visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image125.png"
  o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=580 height=326
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image126.jpg" v:shapes="Image_x0020_41"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt'><span lang=EN-US>You can stop
the generation of simulated datasets by clicking on the &#8220;STOP&#8221;
button. A &#8220;<span class=help-block>Run succeeded</span>&#8221; message
appears when all requested simulations have been processed.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l32 level1 lfo25'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><u><span lang=EN-US>Do not forget to click on
the &#8220;Save&#8221; button in the &#8220;Project administration&#8221; lower
panel to implement and save a concatenated zip file including various input and
output files</span></u><span lang=EN-US> (see section 7 for a description of
the content of some of those files) on your computer. The name of the
implemented/saved concatenated .zip file is the one given at the start in the
&#8220;Project name&#8221; window (here <span class=SpellE>Starting_from_existing_project_IndSeq_demonstration_project</span>).</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:18.0pt'><span style='mso-ansi-language:
FR;mso-fareast-language:FR;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Image_x0020_44"
 o:spid="_x0000_i1038" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:501pt;height:282pt;
 visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image127.png"
  o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=668 height=376
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image128.jpg" v:shapes="Image_x0020_44"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l34 level1 lfo38'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>You might also want to launch
the optional but recommended option &#8220;Prior and scenario checking&#8221;.
For details see section 5.4.7.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l34 level1 lfo38'><a
name="_Toc62127977"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Warning: The button
&#8220;Reset&#8221; at the very bottom part of the &#8220;Project
administration&#8221; panel restart the pipeline from scratch removing all
configurations previously set up and all data and result files generated.</span></a></p>

<h1><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc62127977'><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
"Cambria",serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>6.
PERFORMING RANDOM FOREST ANALYSES</span></span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:"Cambria",serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:
minor-latin'><o:p></o:p></span></h1>

<h2><a name="_Toc62127978"><span lang=EN-US>6.1 Files needed</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoBodyText><span lang=EN-US>Four files are needed at this stage: </span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l28 level1 lfo22'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>the file <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'>headerRF.txt</b> which describes the full settings of the generation of
the training set</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l28 level1 lfo22'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>the training set file <span
class=SpellE><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>reftableRF.bin</b></span>
(generated from the headerRF.txt file), </span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l28 level1 lfo22'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol;color:black;
mso-themecolor:text1'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
lang=EN-US>the file <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>statobsRF.txt</b>
which corresponds to the values of the summary statistics computed for the </span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:
minor-bidi;color:black;mso-themecolor:text1'>observed dataset and which was
generated when producing the headerRF.txt and <span class=SpellE>reftableRF.bin</span>
files.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l28 level1 lfo22'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><u><span lang=EN-US>Warning</span></u><span
lang=EN-US>: although not necessary <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>per
se</i> for Random Forest analyses as the later only need the statobsRF.txt file
as data point to analyze, the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>observed (here
<span class=SpellE>IndSeq</span> SNP) data file</b> has to be present.</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l28 level1 lfo22'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol;color:black;
mso-themecolor:text1'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='color:black;
mso-themecolor:text1'>It is worth stressing that these files are: (<span
class=SpellE>i</span>) already available following an in-course (and
terminated) training set simulation or (ii) they can be selected and loaded
independently by clicking on the &#8220;Existing project&#8221; button and
using the &#8221;Project files&#8221; and &#8220;Data file&#8221; browsers</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='color:black;mso-themecolor:text1'>.</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:
minor-bidi;color:black;mso-themecolor:text1'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:FR'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span></span><span style='mso-ansi-language:
FR;mso-fareast-language:FR;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Image_x0020_71"
