</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=741 height=417
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image130.jpg" v:shapes="Image_x0020_71"><![endif]></span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:
minor-bidi;color:black;mso-themecolor:text1'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc62127979"></a><a name=performing-analyses><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc62127979'><span lang=EN-US>6.2. Scenario choice
analysis</span></span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Click on the large orange color
&#8220;Random Forest Analyses&#8221; button (&#8220;+&#8221; on the right). </span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Click on the button
&#8220;Check input&#8221;: useful information about the training set (cf. <span
class=SpellE>reftableRF.bin</span> file) content is provided (<span
class=SpellE>nbr</span> of scenarios, total <span class=SpellE>nbr</span> of
simulated datasets, <span class=SpellE>nbr</span> of simulated dataset
available per scenario, <span class=SpellE>nbr</span> of parameters, <span
class=SpellE>nbr</span> of summary statistics). </span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText><span style='mso-ansi-language:FR;mso-fareast-language:
FR;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Image_x0020_73" o:spid="_x0000_i1036"
 type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:547.2pt;height:307.8pt;visibility:visible;
 mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image131.png"
  o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=730 height=410
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image132.jpg" v:shapes="Image_x0020_73"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Provide an Analysis
(sub-project) name (here &#8220;<span class=SpellE>Scenario_choice_demonstration</span>&#8221;)
and validate it. </span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Activate the &#8220;Scenario
choice&#8221; button in the mode setting (button activated by default). The
observed dataset that will be analyzed is the one described in the file
&#8220;statobsRF.txt&#8221;.</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText><span style='mso-ansi-language:FR;mso-fareast-language:
FR;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Image_x0020_76" o:spid="_x0000_i1035"
 type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:547.2pt;height:307.8pt;visibility:visible;
 mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image133.png"
  o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=730 height=410
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image134.jpg" v:shapes="Image_x0020_76"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Modify the RF analysis settings
in the following frames or keep default settings</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Indicate the number of samples
(i.e. simulated datasets) in the training set to consider for analyses (default
= 0 = total number of simulated datasets available in the training set). This
number should be lower or equal to the total number of simulated datasets
available in the training set. See section 4.2 for useful insights about this
number.</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Indicate the number of noise
variables to add (default = 5). Noise variables (corresponding to values
randomly drawn into uniform distributions bounded between 0 and 1) allows
evaluating which components of the feature vector (i.e. summary statistics) are
informative (see section 7.3 and Collin et al. 2020 for details).</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Enable/disable the addition of
linear combinations axes (LDA for model choice) (default = enable)</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>You may 'group' your models in
several groups. For instance, if you have six models, labeled from 1 to 6, you
can specify '1,2,3;4,5,6' to make 2 groups of 3. Leave blank to not group
scenarios and analyzed them separately (see Collin et al. 2020). (default =
blank). Note that if you write &#8216;1;3;5&#8217; then the RF scenario choice
analysis will concern only the scenarios 1, 3 and 5 of the training set.</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Indicate the number of tress in
the forest (default = 500). See section 4.3 for useful insights about this
number.</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Click on the button
&#8220;RUN&#8221; to launch the RF analysis for scenario choice </span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText><span style='mso-ansi-language:FR;mso-fareast-language:
FR;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Image_x0020_75" o:spid="_x0000_i1034"
 type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:555.6pt;height:312.6pt;visibility:visible;
 mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image135.png"
  o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=741 height=417
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image136.jpg" v:shapes="Image_x0020_75"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Follow the progress bar. You
can stop the RF analysis by clicking on the &#8220;STOP&#8221; button. A
&#8220;RF run succeeded&#8221; label appears when the RF analysis has been
entirely processed.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Do not forget to click on the
&#8220;Save&#8221; button in the &#8220;Project administration&#8221; panel to
implement and save a concatenated zip file including various input and output
files (see section 7.3 for a description of the content of some of those files)
on your computer. The name of the implemented/saved concatenated zip file is
the one given at the start of the analysis (i.e. Analysis (sub-project) name;
here &#8220;Scenario_choice_demonstration.zip&#8221;).</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Warning: The button
&#8220;Reset&#8221; in the &#8220;Project administration&#8221; panel restart
the pipeline from scratch removing all configurations previously set up and all
data and result files generated.</span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc62127980"><span lang=EN-US>6.3. Parameter estimation analysis</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Click on the large orange color
&#8220;Random Forest Analyses&#8221; button (&#8220;+&#8221; on the right). </span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Activate the &#8220;Parameter
estimation&#8221; button in the mode setting. </span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Click on the button
&#8220;Check input&#8221;: Useful information about the training set (cf. <span
class=SpellE>reftableRF.bin</span> file) content is provided (<span
class=SpellE>nbr</span> of scenarios, total <span class=SpellE>nbr</span> of
simulated datasets, <span class=SpellE>nbr</span> of simulated dataset
available per scenario, <span class=SpellE>nbr</span> of parameters, <span
class=SpellE>nbr</span> of summary statistics). </span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Provide an Analysis
(sub-project) name (here &#8220;<span class=SpellE>Parameter_estimation_ra_demonstration</span>&#8221;)
and validate it. </span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText><span style='mso-ansi-language:FR;mso-fareast-language:
FR;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Image_x0020_78" o:spid="_x0000_i1033"
 type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:555.6pt;height:312.6pt;visibility:visible;
 mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image137.png"
  o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=741 height=417
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image138.jpg" v:shapes="Image_x0020_78"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Activate the &#8220;Parameter
choice&#8221; button in the mode setting. The observed dataset that will be
analyzed is the one described in the file &#8220;statobsRF.txt&#8221;.</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText><span style='mso-ansi-language:FR;mso-fareast-language:
FR;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Image_x0020_79" o:spid="_x0000_i1032"
 type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:555.6pt;height:312.6pt;visibility:visible;
 mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image139.png"
  o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=741 height=417
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image140.jpg" v:shapes="Image_x0020_79"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Indicate the Scenario ID number
for parameter estimation (default = 1)</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Indicate the name of the
parameter to estimate (here the admixture rate &#8220;ra&#8221;): a list of
parameter names available for estimation according to the header and training
set files is provided. Give a single name or a combination of names as
explained in the interface. One analysis has to be processed for each parameter
of interest.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Indicate the number of
simulated datasets in the training set to consider for analyses (default = 0 =
total number of simulated datasets available in the training set). <u>Warning: this
number should be lower or equal to the total number of simulated datasets
available in the training set for the scenario of interest.</u> Here we put
this number to 2000 as only 2028 simulated datasets are available for scenario
3 in the <span class=SpellE>reftableRF.bin</span> file previously used for
scenario choice and also loaded in the present illustration. See section 4.2
for useful insights about the number of simulated datasets in the training set
to consider for parameter estimation. In practice, it might be useful to
generate a (second) training set including only the selected scenario to
process parameter estimation from a larger number of simulated datasets (e.g.
10000 as in Collin et al. 2020).</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Indicate the number of noise
variables to add (default = 5). Noise variables (corresponding to values
randomly drawn into uniform distributions bounded between 0 and 1) allows
evaluating which components of the feature vector (i.e. summary statistics) are
informative (see section 7.3 and Collin et al. 2020 for details).</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph><span style='mso-ansi-language:FR;mso-fareast-language:
FR;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Image_x0020_81" o:spid="_x0000_i1031"
 type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:555.6pt;height:312.6pt;visibility:visible;
 mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image141.png"
  o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=741 height=417
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image142.jpg" v:shapes="Image_x0020_81"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Enable/Disable the addition of linear
combinations axes (PLS for parameter estimation) (default = enable)</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Indicate the threshold of
percentage of explained variance by the PLS components you will keep in the
analysis (default = 0.95)</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Indicate the number of
out-of-bag (<span class=SpellE>oob</span>) testing samples (default = 10 but a
minimum of 1000 <span class=SpellE>oob</span> testing samples is often
necessary to obtained stable estimation of accuracy indices; see section
3.4.2). This number should be equal or lower to the number of datasets
available in the training set for the scenario under study.</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Indicate the number of trees in
the forest &#8211; here 1000 - (default = 500). See section 4.3 for useful
insights about this number.</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Click on the button &#8220;Run&#8221;
to launch the parameter estimation analyses focusing on the single parameter
(or parameter combination) indicated above.</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt'><span style='mso-ansi-language:
FR;mso-fareast-language:FR;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Image_x0020_82"
 o:spid="_x0000_i1030" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:555.6pt;height:312.6pt;
 visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image143.png"
  o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=741 height=417
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image144.jpg" v:shapes="Image_x0020_82"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:
l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Follow the progress bar. You
can stop the RF analysis by clicking on the &#8220;STOP&#8221; button. A
&#8220;RF run succeeded&#8221; label appears when the RF analysis has been
entirely processed.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Do not forget to click on the
&#8220;Save&#8221; button in the &#8220;Project administration&#8221; panel to
implement and save a concatenated zip file including various input and output
files (see section 7.3 for a description of the content of some of those files)
on your computer. The name of the implemented/saved concatenated zip file is
the one given at the start of the analysis (i.e. Analysis (sub-project) name;
here &#8220;Parameter_estimation_ra_demonstration.zip&#8221;).</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l41 level1 lfo23'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Warning: The button
&#8220;Reset&#8221; in the &#8220;Project administration&#8221; panel restart
the pipeline from scratch removing all configurations previously set up and all
data and result files generated.</span></p>

<h1><a name="_Toc62127981"><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Cambria",serif;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>7. KEY FILES</span></a><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Cambria",serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'><o:p></o:p></span></h1>

<p class=FirstParagraph><span lang=EN-US>The program uses and produces various
files which we will describe now.</span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc62127982"><span lang=EN-US>7.1 Data files</span></a><span
lang=EN-US> </span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:
0cm;margin-left:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-pagination:widow-orphan lines-together;
page-break-after:avoid;mso-outline-level:2'><a name="_Toc62127983"><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-fareast;
mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-bidi;color:#4F81BD;
mso-themecolor:accent1'>7.1.1 </span></b></a><span class=SpellE><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc62127983'><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-bidi;
color:#4F81BD;mso-themecolor:accent1'>IndSeq</span></b></span></span><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc62127983'><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-bidi;
color:#4F81BD;mso-themecolor:accent1'> SNP data</span></b></span><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-fareast;
mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-bidi;color:#4F81BD;
mso-themecolor:accent1'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=FirstParagraph><span lang=EN-US>The data file format includes:</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:24.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>A first line (headline)
providing the sex-ratio as above (e.g. </span><!--[if gte msEquation 12]><m:oMath><i
 style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Cambria Math",serif'><m:r>NM</m:r><m:r>=1.0</m:r><m:r>NF</m:r><m:r>&gt;</m:r></span></i></m:oMath><![endif]--><![if !msEquation]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-bidi;position:relative;top:2.5pt;mso-text-raise:-2.5pt;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="_x0000_i1025" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:79.8pt;height:13.8pt'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image145.png"
  o:title="" chromakey="white"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=106 height=18
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image146.gif" v:shapes="_x0000_i1025"><![endif]></span><![endif]><span
lang=EN-US>), the required MAF (minimum allele frequency criterion; e.g.
MAF=0.05 or MAF=hudson&gt;), and any text that can be used as a title. The sex
ratio of the analyzed species is noted under the form &lt;NM=<span
class=SpellE>rNF</span>&gt;, in which r is the ratio of the number of females
per male (e.g. &lt;NM=2.5NF&gt; means that the number of males is 2.5 times the
number of females; for a balanced sex ratio one should write &lt;NM=1.0NF&gt;).
The MAF is computed pooling all genes genotyped over all studied population
samples. For instance, the specification of a MAF equal to 5% (i.e. MAF=0.05)
will automatically select a subset of m loci characterized by a minimum allele
frequency 5% among the <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>l</i> locus of the
observed dataset. In agreement with this, only <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:
normal'>m</i> locus with a MAF&gt;5%. Writing &lt;MAF = Hudson&gt; (or omitting
to write any instruction with respect to the MAF) will bring the program to use
the standard Hudson&#8217;s algorithm without further selection; see also the
above section 2.4.2.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:24.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>A second line starting with the
three keywords </span><span class=VerbatimChar><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'>IND SEX POP</span></span><span
lang=EN-US>, separated by at least one space, followed by as many letters as
SNP loci, the letter giving the location of the locus as above <i
style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>A</i> for autosomal diploid loci, <i
style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>H</i> for autosomal haploid loci, <i
style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>X</i> for X-linked (or haplo-diploid) loci,<i
style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'> Y</i> for Y-linked loci and <i
style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>M</i> for mitochondrial loci. Letters are
separated by a single space.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:24.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>As many lines as there are
genotyped individuals, with the code-name of the individual, a letter (M or F;
or 9 if the sex of the individual is unknown) indicating its sex, and a
code-name for its population. <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><u>A
genotype is defined by the values 0, 1 or 2 which correspond to the number of
the (arbitrarily chosen) reference allele composing the genotype</u></b><u> </u>at
each SNP locus. For instance, in the case autosomal diploid SNP loci (denoted
A), we have: 2 = homozygous genotype for the reference allele (cf. 2 copies of
the reference allele), 1 = heterozygous genotype (cf. 1 copy of the reference
allele), and 0 = homozygous genotype for the variant allele, with 0 copy of the
reference allele. <u>It is worth noting that for autosomal haploid loci
(denoted H), as well as for mitochondrial loci (denoted M) and Y-linked loci
(denoted Y), the SNP genotypes will be 0 or 1, which is coherent with our logic
of defining a genotype according to the number of the reference allele
composing the genotype.<o:p></o:p></u></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:24.0pt;mso-add-space:auto;
text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Missing SNP genotypes are noted
9 for all type of SNP loci.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:24.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Only a subset of the SNP loci
included in the data file can be considered (selected) in the simulations and
hence in subsequent analyses, without modifying the original dataset. For
instance, one can choose to select in the corresponding panel the SNP loci 1 to
1000 of a data file including a total of say 10000 loci (see the above section
5.4.4). This allows running faster simulations and processing independent replicate
analyses of sets of 1000 SNP loci by considering loci 1 to 1000 and then 1001
to 2000, and so on, in separate analyses.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:24.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Following Hudson&#8217;s (2002)
criterion, only polymorphic SNP loci (over the entire dataset) are considered.
Monomorphic SNP loci (over the entire dataset) are automatically filtered by
the program. It is preferable, however, that the user removes himself all
monomorphic loci from his/her (observed) dataset before submitting it to DIYABC
Random Forest.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:24.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Before running any simulation,
DIYABC Random Forest provides a text file including the set of SNP loci
selected from the observed dataset (e.g. polymorphic loci 1 to 1000 with a
MAF=0.05). This file is named &#8220;UserDataFileName.bin.txt&#8221;.</span></p>

<p class=FirstParagraph><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
lang=EN-US>EXAMPLE<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText><span lang=EN-US>In our example below, the species is
diploid, has an unbalanced sex ration the sex-ratio as above (i.e.
&lt;NM=1.5NF&gt;) and two of its populations were genotyped at 23 SNP loci: 20
autosomal loci, 1 X-linked locus, 1 Y-linked locus and 1 mitochondrial locus. The
first line provides the title which includes the species sex-ratio and the MAF
(minimum allele frequency). The second line indicates: individual name in
column 1, individual sex in column 2 (</span><span class=VerbatimChar><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'>M</span></span><span
lang=EN-US> for male, </span><span class=VerbatimChar><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'>F</span></span><span
lang=EN-US> for female, </span><span class=VerbatimChar><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'>9</span></span><span
lang=EN-US> or any other letter if unknown), population name in column 3 and
one column per SNP locus (letter </span><span class=VerbatimChar><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'>A</span></span><span
lang=EN-US> for an autosomal locus, </span><span class=VerbatimChar><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'>X</span></span><span
lang=EN-US> for an X-linked locus, </span><span class=VerbatimChar><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'>Y</span></span><span
lang=EN-US> for a Y-linked locus and </span><span class=VerbatimChar><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'>M</span></span><span
lang=EN-US> for a mitochondrial locus). Columns are separated by one or more
spaces. SNP genotypes are coded </span><span class=VerbatimChar><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'>0</span></span><span
lang=EN-US>, </span><span class=VerbatimChar><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'>1</span></span><span lang=EN-US> or </span><span
class=VerbatimChar><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
12.0pt'>2</span></span><span lang=EN-US> (</span><span class=VerbatimChar><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'>9</span></span><span
lang=EN-US> for missing data) according to the number of reference alleles at
the corresponding locus. Note that the sex has no influence on simulations for
autosomal, mitochondrial or haploid loci (any sex can be hence declared). For
individuals with an unknown sex (denoted </span><span class=VerbatimChar><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'>9</span></span><span
lang=EN-US>, see </span><span class=VerbatimChar><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'>IND P1_2, P1_3 and P2_15),</span></span><span
lang=EN-US> data for autosomal (as well as mitochondrial and haploid) loci will
be <span class=GramE>taken into account</span> and simulated. On the other
hand, the genotypes of X-linked and Y-linked loci for the </span><span
class=VerbatimChar><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
12.0pt'>same IND P1_2, P1_3 and P2_15</span></span><span lang=EN-US> with unknown
sex cannot be safely determined and are hence noted </span><span
class=VerbatimChar><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
12.0pt'>9</span></span><span lang=EN-US> for missing data (i.e. they are not
simulated).</span></p>

<p class=CaptionedFigure><span style='mso-ansi-language:FR;mso-fareast-language:
FR;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Image14" o:spid="_x0000_i1029"
 type="#_x0000_t75" alt="image" style='width:348pt;height:313.2pt;visibility:visible;
 mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image147.png"
  o:title="image"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=464 height=418
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image148.jpg" alt=image
v:shapes="Image14"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:
0cm;margin-left:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-pagination:widow-orphan lines-together;
page-break-after:avoid;mso-outline-level:2'><a name="_Toc62127984"><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-fareast;
mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-bidi;color:#4F81BD;
mso-themecolor:accent1'>7.1.2 </span></b></a><span class=SpellE><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc62127984'><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-bidi;
color:#4F81BD;mso-themecolor:accent1'>PoolSeq</span></b></span></span><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc62127984'><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-bidi;
color:#4F81BD;mso-themecolor:accent1'> SNP data</span></b></span><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-fareast;
mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-bidi;color:#4F81BD;
mso-themecolor:accent1'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=FirstParagraph><span lang=EN-US>The data file format includes:</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:24.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>A first line (headline)
providing the sex-ratio of the analyzed species (e.g.&lt;NM=1.0NF&gt;), the required
MRC (minimum read count criterion; e.g. &lt;MRC=5&gt;), and any text that can
be used as a title. The sex ratio is noted under the form &lt;NM=<span
class=SpellE>rNF</span>&gt;, in which r is the ratio of the number of females
per male (e.g. &lt;NM=2.5NF&gt; means that the number of males is 2.5 times the
number of females; for a balanced sex ratio one should write &lt;NM=1.0NF&gt;).
The MRC is the number of sequence reads of the minor allele frequency allele
when pooling the reads <span class=SpellE>over all</span> population samples.
The specification of a MRC equal for instance to 5 (as in the present example)
will automatically select a subset of <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>m</i>
<span class=SpellE>PoolSeq</span> loci characterized by more than five reads
over all studied pools among the l loci of the observed dataset. For instance,
the first locus of the list (cf. third line of the file) will not be selected.
In agreement with this, only <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>m</i> loci
with more than five reads will be retained in a simulated dataset. We advise
using MRC values of 2, 3, 4 or 5.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:24.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Remember that (in contrast to <span
class=SpellE>IndSeq</span> SNP) only <span class=SpellE>PoolSeq</span> SNPs
located on autosomal chromosomes of diploid individuals can be considered by
the program.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:24.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>A second line provides the
haploid sample size of each population pool.<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:24.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>The following lines correspond
to the <span class=SpellE>PoolSeq</span> SNP genotypes (given in read counts).
Each line represents a SNP and each pair of columns points to a population pool
</span><span class=tlid-translation><span lang=EN style='mso-ansi-language:
EN'>in the same order as in the second line</span></span><span lang=EN-US>. For
each SNP-pool combination, the number of read counts is indicated for the first
and second allele in the first and second column, respectively. </span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:24.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:
l0 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;
mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Warning: no missing data (i.e.
&#8220;0 0&#8221; data; cf. no read count for any allele) is allowed in the <span
class=SpellE>PoolSeq</span> data file and this for any pools in the data file.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:24.0pt;mso-add-space:auto;
text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>We advise to put only SNP loci
with a coverage &gt; 10 reads for each analyzed pool of the dataset in order to
ensure descent allele frequency estimation within each pool. SNP loci with an
abnormally high coverage should be also removed as those loci can be duplicated
loci.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:24.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Only a subset of the SNP loci
included in the data file can be considered (selected) in the simulations and
hence in subsequent analyses, without modifying the original dataset. For
instance, one can choose to select in the corresponding panel the SNP loci 1 to
1000 of a data file including a total of say 10000 loci (see the above section
5.4.4). This allows running faster simulations and processing independent
replicate analyses of sets of 1000 SNP loci by considering loci 1 to 1000 and
then 1001 to 2000, and so on, in separate analyses.</span></p>

<p class=FirstParagraph><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
lang=EN-US>EXAMPLE<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText><span lang=EN-US>In our example below, the species is
diploid and was genotyped using the <span class=SpellE>PoolSeq</span>
technology at several thousands of autosomal SNPs in four population pools; <u>only
the first 13 SNPs are shown here </u>for sake of concision.<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>The species sex-ratio is balanced and
hence equal 1 and the MRC (minimum read count) is 5. Each population pool is
composed of 100 diploid individuals (haploid sample size = 200).<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>The second line provides the haploid
sample size of each population pool. It has to start with the explicit
terminology POOL POP_NAME:HAPLOID_SAMPLE_SIZE. Here the haploid sample size is
200 for each &#8220;<span class=SpellE>POPx</span>&#8221;. Note that you can
write any sample name, e.g. MONTPELLIER, instead of <span class=SpellE>POPx</span>.<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>Columns are separated by one or more
spaces. Each line represents a SNP (hence the 13 lines) and each pair of
columns points to a population pool (hence the 4 pairs of <span class=GramE>column</span>).
For each SNP-pool combination, the number of read counts is indicated for the
first and second allele in the first and second column, respectively. For
instance, we have 2 reads of the first allele and 114 reads of the second
allele for the first SNP genotyped in the POOL-POP3. Note that because the
MRC=5 several SNP of the present example data file, e.g. the first SNP for
which only two read counts are present over all pools, will not be selected
when generating simulated datasets.</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText><span style='mso-ansi-language:FR;mso-fareast-language:
FR;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Picture_x0020_4" o:spid="_x0000_i1028"
 type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:469.8pt;height:313.2pt;visibility:visible;
 mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image149.emz"
  o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=626 height=418
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image150.gif" v:shapes="Picture_x0020_4"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:10.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:
0cm;margin-left:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-pagination:widow-orphan lines-together;
page-break-after:avoid;mso-outline-level:2'><a name="_Toc62127985"><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-fareast;
mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-bidi;color:#4F81BD;
mso-themecolor:accent1'>7.1.3 Microsatellite and DNA sequence data</span></b></a><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-fareast;
mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-bidi;color:#4F81BD;
mso-themecolor:accent1'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=FirstParagraph><span lang=EN-US>The data file format is an extended
format of the file used in the classical population genetics program <span
class=SpellE>Genepop</span> (<span class=SpellE>Rousset</span> et al. 1995).
The additional features are:</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l21 level1 lfo29'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>In the title line appears the
sex ratio noted </span><!--[if gte msEquation 12]><m:oMath><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:
 normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Cambria Math",serif'><m:r>NM</m:r><m:r>=</m:r><m:r>rNF</m:r><m:r>&gt;</m:r></span></i></m:oMath><![endif]--><![if !msEquation]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-bidi;position:relative;top:2.5pt;mso-text-raise:-2.5pt;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="_x0000_i1025" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:69.6pt;height:13.8pt'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image151.png"
  o:title="" chromakey="white"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=93 height=18
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image152.gif" v:shapes="_x0000_i1025"><![endif]></span><![endif]><span
lang=EN-US>, in which </span><!--[if gte msEquation 12]><m:oMath><i
 style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Cambria Math",serif'><m:r>r</m:r></span></i></m:oMath><![endif]--><![if !msEquation]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-bidi;position:relative;top:2.5pt;mso-text-raise:-2.5pt;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape

 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image021.png"
  o:title="" chromakey="white"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=8 height=18
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image022.gif" v:shapes="_x0000_i1025"><![endif]></span><![endif]><span
lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span>is the ratio of the
number of females per male (</span><!--[if gte msEquation 12]><m:oMath><i
 style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Cambria Math",serif'><m:r>e</m:r><m:r>.</m:r><m:r>g</m:r><m:r>.</m:r></span></i></m:oMath><![endif]--><![if !msEquation]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:

mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";

 id="_x0000_i1025" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:20.4pt;height:13.8pt'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image153.png"
  o:title="" chromakey="white"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=27 height=18
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image154.gif" v:shapes="_x0000_i1025"><![endif]></span><![endif]><span
lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span></span><!--[if gte msEquation 12]><m:oMath><i
 style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Cambria Math",serif'><m:r>NM</m:r><m:r>=2.5</m:r><m:r>NF</m:r><m:r>&gt;</m:r></span></i></m:oMath><![endif]--><![if !msEquation]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-bidi;position:relative;top:2.5pt;mso-text-raise:-2.5pt;

 id="_x0000_i1025" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:79.8pt;height:13.8pt'>
 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image155.png"
  o:title="" chromakey="white"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=106 height=18

lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span>means that the number of
males is 2.5 times the number of females; for a balanced sex ratio one should
write </span><!--[if gte msEquation 12]><m:oMath><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:

lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:

mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";

 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image145.png"
  o:title="" chromakey="white"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=106 height=18
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image146.gif" v:shapes="_x0000_i1025"><![endif]></span><![endif]><span
lang=EN-US>). Since the title is generally only copied, this addition should
not interfere with other programs using Genepop datafiles. <span class=GramE>Also</span>
if there is no such sex ratio addition, DIYABC will consider by default that
NM=1.0NF.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l21 level1 lfo29'><![if !supportLists]><span

</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>After the locus name, there is
an indication for the category of the locus which is </span><!--[if gte msEquation 12]><m:oMath><i

mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";

  o:title="" chromakey="white"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=26 height=18

lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span>for Y-linked loci and </span><!--[if gte msEquation 12]><m:oMath><i
 style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Cambria Math",serif'><m:r>M</m:r><m:r>&gt;</m:r></span></i></m:oMath><![endif]--><![if !msEquation]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:

mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-bidi;position:relative;top:2.5pt;mso-text-raise:-2.5pt;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape

 <v:imagedata src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image165.png"
  o:title="" chromakey="white"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=30 height=18
src="DiyabcRandomForestUserManual21-01-2021_fichiers/image166.gif" v:shapes="_x0000_i1025"><![endif]></span><![endif]><span
lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span>for mitochondrial loci.
If no category is noted, DIYABC will consider the locus as autosomal diploid or
autosomal haploid depending on the corresponding genotype of the first typed
individual.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l21 level1 lfo29'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Genotypes of microsatellite
loci are noted with <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>six digit numbers</b>
if diploid (e.g.&nbsp;190188 for a heterozygous genotype with one allele 190
and one allele 188, and 200200 for a homozygous genotype with two alleles 200)
and by <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>three digit numbers</b>
(e.g.&nbsp;190) if haploid. <u>The three digit numbers correspond to the length
in nucleotides of the corresponding PCR products</u>.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:35.7pt;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-17.85pt;mso-list:l21 level1 lfo29'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Sequence locus are noted
between &lt; and &gt;. In addition, each sequence alleles/haplotypes <span
class=GramE>is</span> noted between brackets. For instance, a haploid sequence
locus will be noted &lt;[GTCTA]&gt; and a diploid sequence locus &lt;[GTCTA][GTCTT]&gt;.
Sequences may contain undetermined nucleotides which will be denoted &quot;N
&quot; or &quot; - &quot;. Note that all sequence alleles/haplotypes have to be
of same length. The length of shorter sequence allele/haplotypes needs to be
adjusted to the larger sequence allele/haplotype by adding &quot;N &quot; or
&quot; - &quot; symbols at the end of the sequences. It is worth stressing
that, at a given locus, only the portion of the sequence shared by all
individuals of the dataset will be used for computing summary statistics. We
therefore advise removing locus-individual sequence data with too many
&#8220;N&#8221; and replace them by missing data. Finally, remember that this
version of the program does not consider insertion-deletion mutations, mainly
because there does not seem to be much consensus on this topic.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:35.7pt;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-17.85pt;mso-list:l21 level1 lfo29'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Missing microsatellite
genotypes are noted 000 if haploid or 000000 if diploid.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:35.7pt;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-17.85pt;mso-list:l21 level1 lfo29'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Missing sequence
alleles/haplotypes are noted <span class=GramE>&lt;[</span> ]&gt; if haploid or
&lt;[ ][ ]&gt; if diploid.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-left:35.7pt;mso-add-space:auto;
text-indent:-17.85pt;mso-list:l21 level1 lfo29'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>&middot;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Missing data are <span
class=GramE>taken into account</span> in the following way. For each appearance
of a missing genotype in the observed dataset, the program records the
individual and the locus. When simulating datasets, the program replaces the
simulated genotype (obtained through the coalescence process algorithm) by the
missing data code at all corresponding locations. All summary statistics are
thus computed with the same missing data as for the observed dataset. <i
style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>WARNING</i>: data files with virtually any
amount of missing data can be analyzed by DIYABC Random Forest. <u>However, for
each locus a minimum of one genotyped individual per population is required.</u>
This is because summary statistics cannot be computed at a given locus in a
given population if only missing data are present.</span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US>EXAMPLES<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText><u><span lang=EN-US>Example 1</span></u><span lang=EN-US>:<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>the example dataset below includes two
population samples, each of 12 diploid individuals (8 females and 4 males in
the first sample and 5 females and 7 males in the second sample). As deduced
from the letter between<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>and<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>on the locus name lines (see page 25),
these individuals have been genotyped at 3 microsatellite loci (1 autosomal </span><!--[if gte msEquation 12]><m:oMath><i

lang=EN-US>, 1 X-linked </span><!--[if gte msEquation 12]><m:oMath><i

<p class=MsoBodyText><a name="_Toc62034937"><span style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoBodyText><u><span lang=EN-US>Example 2</span></u><span lang=EN-US>:

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='mso-ansi-language:FR;mso-fareast-language:FR;
